<s> THE GREEN FLAG When Jack Conolly, of the Irish Shotgun Brigade, the Rory of the Hills Inner Circle, and the extreme left wing of the Land League, was incontinently shot by Sergeant Murdoch of the constabulary, in a little moonlight frolic near Kanturk, his twin-brother Dennis joined the British Army </s>
<s> The countryside had become too hot for him; and, as the seventy-five shillings were wanting which might have carried him to America, he took the only way handy of getting himself out of the way </s>
<s> Seldom has Her Majesty had a less promising recruit, for his hot Celtic blood seethed with hatred against Britain and all things British </s>
<s> The sergeant, however, smiling complacently over his 6 ft </s>
<s> of brawn and his 44 in </s>
<s> chest, whisked him off with a dozen other of the boys to the depot at Fermoy, whence in a few weeks they were sent on, with the spade-work kinks taken out of their backs, to the first battalion of the Royal Mallows, at the top of the roster for foreign service </s>
<s> The Royal Mallows, at about that date, were as strange a lot of men as ever were paid by a great empire to fight its battles </s>
<s> It was the darkest hour of the land struggle, when the one side came out with crow-bar and battering-ram by day, and the other with mask and with shot-gun by night </s>
<s> Men driven from their homes and potato-patches found their way even into the service of the Government, to which it seemed to them that they owed their troubles, and now and then they did wild things before they came </s>
<s> There were recruits in the Irish regiments who would forget to answer to their own names, so short had been their acquaintance with them </s>
<s> Of these the Royal Mallows had their full share; and, while they still retained their fame as being one of the smartest corps in the army, no one knew better than their officers that they were dry-rotted with treason and with bitter hatred of the flag under which they served </s>
<s> And the centre of all the disaffection was C Company, in which Dennis Conolly found himself enrolled </s>
<s> They were Celts, Catholics, and men of the tenant class to a man; and their whole experience of the British Government had been an inexorable landlord, and a constabulary who seemed to them to be always on the side of the rent-collector </s>
<s> Dennis was not the only moonlighter in the ranks, nor was he alone in having an intolerable family blood-feud to harden his heart </s>
<s> Savagery had begotten savagery in that veiled civil war </s>
<s> A landlord with an iron mortgage weighing down upon him had small bowels for his tenantry </s>
<s> He did but take what the law allowed, and yet, with men like Jim Holan, or Patrick McQuire, or Peter Flynn, who had seen the roofs torn from their cottages and their folk huddled among their pitiable furniture upon the roadside, it was ill to argue about abstract law </s>
<s> What matter that in that long and bitter struggle there was many another outrage on the part of the tenant, and many another grievance on the side of the landowner </s>
<s> A stricken man can only feel his own wound, and the rank and file of the C Company of the Royal Mallows were sore and savage to the soul </s>
<s> There were low whisperings in barrack-rooms and canteens, stealthy meetings in public-house parlours, bandying of passwords from mouth to mouth, and many other signs which made their officers right glad when the order came which sent them to foreign, and better still, to active service </s>
<s> For Irish regiments have before now been disaffected, and have at a distance looked upon the foe as though he might, in truth, be the friend; but when they have been put face on to him, and when their officers have dashed to the front with a wave and halloo, those rebel hearts have softened and their gallant Celtic blood has boiled with the mad Joy of the fight, until the slower Britons have marvelled that they ever could have doubted the loyalty of their Irish comrades </s>
<s> So it would be again, according to the officers, and so it would not be if Dennis Conolly and a few others could have their way </s>
<s> It was a March morning upon the eastern fringe of the Nubian desert </s>
<s> The sun had not yet risen, but a tinge of pink flushed up as far as the cloudless zenith, and the long strip of sea lay like a rosy ribbon across the horizon </s>
<s> From the coast inland stretched dreary sand-plains, dotted over with thick clumps at mimosa scrub and mottled patches of thorny bush </s>
<s> No tree broke the monotony of that vast desert </s>
<s> The dull, dusty hue of the thickets, and the yellow glare of the sand, were the only colours, save at one point, where, from a distance, it seemed that a land-slip of snow-white stones had shot itself across a low foot-hill </s>
<s> But as the traveller approached he saw, with a thrill, that these were no stones, but the bleaching bones of a slaughtered army </s>
<s> With its dull tints, its gnarled, viprous bushes, its arid, barren soil, and this death streak trailed across it, it was indeed a nightmare country </s>
<s> Some eight or ten miles inland the rolling plain curved upwards with a steeper slope until it ran into a line of red basaltic rock which zigzagged from north to south, heaping itself up at one point into a fantastic knoll </s>
<s> On the summit of this there stood upon that March morning three Arab chieftains--the Sheik Kadra of the Hadendowas, Moussa Wad Aburhegel, who led the Berber dervishes, and Hamid Wad Hussein, who had come northward with his fighting men from the land of the Baggaras </s>
<s> They had all three just risen from their praying-carpets, and were peering out, with fierce, high-nosed faces thrust forwards, at the stretch of country revealed by the spreading dawn </s>
<s> The red rim of the sun was pushing itself now above the distant sea, and the whole coast-line stood out brilliantly yellow against the rich deep blue beyond </s>
<s> At one spot lay a huddle of white-walled houses, a mere splotch in the distance; while four tiny cock-boats, which lay beyond, marked the position of three of Her Majesty's 10,000-ton troopers and the admiral's flagship </s>
<s> But it was not upon the distant town, nor upon the great vessels, nor yet upon the sinister white litter which gleamed in the plain beneath them, that the Arab chieftains gazed </s>
<s> Two miles from where they stood, amid the sand-hills and the mimosa scrub, a great parallelogram had been marked by piled-up bushes </s>
<s> From the inside of this dozens of tiny blue smoke-reeks curled up into the still morning air; while there rose from it a confused deep murmur, the voices of men and the gruntings of camels blended into the same insect buzz </s>
<s> "The unbelievers have cooked their morning food," said the Baggara chief, shading his eyes with his tawny, sinewy hand </s>
<s> "Truly their sleep has been scanty; for Hamid and a hundred of his men have fired upon them since the rising of the moon" </s>
<s> "So it was with these others," answered the Sheik Kadra, pointing with his sheathed sword towards the old battle-field </s>
<s> "They also had a day of little water and a night of little rest, and the heart was gone out of them ere ever the sons of the Prophet had looked them in the eyes </s>
<s> This blade drank deep that day, and will again before the sun has travelled from the sea to the hill" </s>
<s> "And yet these are other men," remarked the Berber dervish </s>
<s> "Well, I know that Allah has placed them in the clutch of our fingers, yet it may be that they with the big hats will stand firmer than the cursed men of Egypt" </s>
<s> "Pray Allah that it may be so," cried the fierce Baggara, with a flash of his black eyes </s>
<s> "It was not to chase women that I brought 700 men from the river to the coast </s>
<s> See, my brother, already they are forming their array" </s>
<s> A fanfare of bugle-calls burst from the distant camp </s>
<s> At the same time the bank of bushes at one side had been thrown or trampled down, and the little army within began to move slowly out on to the plain </s>
<s> Once clear of the camp they halted, and the slant rays of the sun struck flashes from bayonet and from gun-barrel as the ranks closed up until the big pith helmets joined into a single long white ribbon </s>
<s> Two streaks of scarlet glowed on either side of the square, but elsewhere the fringe of fighting-men was of the dull yellow khaki tint which hardly shows against the desert sand </s>
<s> Inside their array was a dense mass of camels and mules bearing stores and ambulance needs </s>
<s> Outside a twinkling clump of cavalry was drawn up on each flank, and in front a thin, scattered line of mounted infantry was already slowly advancing over the bush-strewn plain, halting on every eminence, and peering warily round as men might who have to pick their steps among the bones of those who have preceded them </s>
<s> The three chieftains still lingered upon the knoll, looking down with hungry eyes and compressed lips at the dark steel-tipped patch </s>
<s> "They are slower to start than the men of Egypt," the Sheik of the Hadendowas growled in his beard </s>
<s> "Slower also to go back, perchance, my brother," murmured the dervish </s>
<s> "And yet they are not many--3,000 at the most" </s>
<s> "And we 10,000, with the Prophet's grip upon our spear-hafts and his words upon our banner </s>
<s> See to their chieftain, how he rides upon the right and looks up at us with the glass that sees from afar </s>
<s> It may be that he sees this also" </s>
<s> The Arab shook his sword at the small clump of horsemen who had spurred out from the square </s>
<s> "Lo </s>
<s> he beckons," cried the dervish; "and see those others at the corner, how they bend and heave </s>
<s> Ha </s>
<s> by the Prophet, I had thought it" </s>
<s> As he spoke, a little woolly puff of smoke spurted up at the corner of the square, and a 7 lb </s>
<s> shell burst with a hard metallic smack just over their heads </s>
<s> The splinters knocked chips from the red rocks around them </s>
<s> "Bismillah" </s>
<s> cried the Hadendowa; "if the gun can carry thus far, then ours can answer to it </s>
<s> Ride to the left, Moussa, and tell Ben Ali to cut the skin from the Egyptians if they cannot hit yonder mark </s>
<s> And you, Hamid, to the right, and see that 3,000 men lie close in the wady that we have chosen </s>
<s> Let the others beat the drum and show the banner of the Prophet, for by the black stone their spears will have drunk deep ere they look upon the stars again" </s>
<s> A long, straggling, boulder-strewn plateau lay on the summit of the red hills, sloping very precipitously to the plain, save at one point, where a winding gully curved downwards, its mouth choked with sand-mounds and olive-hued scrub </s>
<s> Along the edge of this position lay the Arab host--a motley crew of shock-headed desert clansmen, fierce predatory slave dealers of the interior, and wild dervishes from the Upper Nile, all blent together by their common fearlessness and fanaticism </s>
<s> Two races were there, as wide as the poles apart--the thin-lipped, straight-haired Arab and the thick-lipped, curly negro--yet the faith of Islam had bound them closer than a blood tie </s>
<s> Squatting among the rocks, or lying thickly in the shadow, they peered out at the slow-moving square beneath them, while women with water-skins and bags of dhoora fluttered from group to group, calling out to each other those fighting texts from the Koran which in the hour of battle are maddening as wine to the true believer </s>
<s> A score of banners waved over the ragged, valiant crew, and among them, upon desert horses and white Bishareen camels, were the Emirs and Sheiks who were to lead them against the infidels </s>
<s> As the Sheik Kadra sprang into his saddle and drew his sword there was a wild whoop and a clatter of waving spears, while the one-ended war-drums burst into a dull crash like a wave upon shingle </s>
<s> For a moment 10,000 men were up on the rocks with brandished arms and leaping figures; the next they were under cover again, waiting sternly and silently for their chieftain's orders </s>
<s> The square was less than half a mile from the ridge now, and shell after shell from the 7 lb </s>
<s> guns were pitching over it </s>
<s> A deep roar on the right, and then a second one showed that the Egyptian Krupps were in action </s>
<s> Sheik Kadra's hawk eyes saw that the shells burst far beyond the mark, and he spurred his horse along to where a knot of mounted chiefs were gathered round the two guns, which were served by their captured crews </s>
<s> "How is this, Ben Ali" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "It was not thus that the dogs fired when it was their own brothers in faith at whom they aimed" </s>
<s> A chieftain reined his horse back, and thrust a blood-smeared sword into its sheath </s>
<s> Beside him two Egyptian artillerymen with their throats cut were sobbing out their lives upon the ground </s>
<s> "Who lays the gun this time" </s>
<s> asked the fierce chief, glaring at the frightened gunners" </s>
<s> Here, thou black-browed child of Shaitan, aim, and aim for thy life" </s>
<s> It may have been chance, or it may have been skill, but the third and fourth shells burst over the square </s>
<s> Sheik Kadra smiled grimly and galloped back to the left, where his spearmen were streaming down into the gully </s>
<s> As he joined them a deep growling rose from the plain beneath, like the snarling of a sullen wild beast, and a little knot of tribesmen fell into a struggling heap, caught in the blast of lead from a Gardner </s>
<s> Their comrades pressed on over them, and sprang down into the ravine </s>
<s> From all along the crest burst the hard, sharp crackle of Remington fire </s>
<s> The square had slowly advanced, rippling over the low sandhills, and halting every few minutes to re-arrange its formation </s>
<s> Now, having made sure that there was no force of the enemy in the scrub, it changed its direction, and began to take a line parallel to the Arab position </s>
<s> It was too steep to assail from the front, and if they moved far enough to the right the general hoped that he might turn it </s>
<s> On the top of those ruddy hills lay a baronetcy for him, and a few extra hundreds in his pension, and he meant having them both that day </s>
<s> The Remington fire was annoying, and so were those two Krupp guns; already there were more cacolets full than he cared to see </s>
<s> But on the whole he thought it better to hold his fire until he had more to aim at than a few hundred of fuzzy heads peeping over a razor-back ridge </s>
<s> He was a bulky, red-faced man, a fine whist-player, and a soldier who knew his work </s>
<s> His men believed in him, and he had good reason to believe in them, for he had excellent stuff under him that day </s>
<s> Being an ardent champion of the short-service system, he took particular care to work with veteran first battalions, and his little force was the compressed essence of an army corps </s>
<s> The left front of the square was formed by four companies of the Royal Wessex, and the right by four of the Royal Mallows </s>
<s> On either side the other halves of the same regiments marched in quarter column of companies </s>
<s> Behind them, on the right was a battalion of Guards, and on the left one of Marines, while the rear was closed in by a Rifle battalion </s>
<s> Two Royal Artillery 7 lb </s>
<s> screw-guns kept pace with the square, and a dozen white-bloused sailors, under their blue-coated, tight-waisted officers, trailed their Gardner in front, turning every now and then to spit up at the draggled banners which waved over the cragged ridge </s>
<s> Hussars and Lancers scouted in the scrub at each side, and within moved the clump of camels, with humorous eyes and supercilious lips, their comic faces a contrast to the blood-stained men who already lay huddled in the cacolets on either side </s>
<s> The square was now moving slowly on a line parallel with the rocks, stopping every few minutes to pick up wounded, and to allow the screw-guns and Gardner to make themselves felt </s>
<s> The men looked serious, for that spring on to the rocks of the Arab army had given them a vague glimpse of the number and ferocity of their foes; but their faces were set like stone, for they knew to a man that they must win or they must die--and die, too, in a particularly unlovely fashion </s>
<s> But most serious of all was the general, for he had seen that which brought a flush to his cheeks and a frown to his brow </s>
<s> "I say, Stephen," said he to his galloper, "those Mallows seem a trifle jumpy </s>

<s> The colonel, a fine old Celtic warrior, was over at C Company in an instant </s>
<s> "How are the men, Captain Foley" </s>

<s> "Stiffen them up" </s>
<s> cried the colonel </s>

<s> In their march in front of what looked like a face of cliff, they had come opposite to the mouth of the gully, in which, screened by scrub and boulders, 3,000 chosen dervishes, under Hamid Wad Hussein, of the Baggaras, were crouching </s>

<s> CAPTAIN SHARKEY </s>
<s> I HOW THE GOVERNOR OF SAINT KITT'S CAME HOME </s>
<s> When the great wars of the Spanish Succession had been brought to an end by the Treaty of Utrecht, the vast number of privateers which had been fitted out by the contending parties found their occupation gone </s>
<s> Some took to the more peaceful but less lucrative ways of ordinary commerce, others were absorbed into the fishing fleets, and a few of the more reckless hoisted the Jolly Rodger at the mizzen, and the bloody flag at the main, declaring a private war upon their own account against the whole human race </s>
<s> With mixed crews, recruited from every nation, they scoured the seas, disappearing occasionally to careen in some lonely inlet, or putting in for a debauch at some outlying port, where they dazzled the inhabitants by their lavishness, and horrified them by their brutalities </s>
<s> On the Coromandel Coast, at Madagascar, in the African waters, and above all in the West Indian and American seas, the pirates were a constant menace </s>
<s> With an insolent luxury they would regulate their depredations by the comfort of the seasons, harrying New England in the summer, and dropping south again to the tropical islands in the winter </s>
<s> They were the more to be dreaded because they had none of that discipline and restraint which made their predecessors, the Buccaneers, both formidable and respectable </s>
<s> These Ishmaels of the sea rendered an account to no man, and treated their prisoners according to the drunken whim of the moment </s>
<s> Flashes of grotesque generosity alternated with longer stretches of inconceivable ferocity, and the skipper who fell into their hands might find himself dismissed with his cargo, after serving as boon companion in some hideous debauch, or might sit at his cabin table with his own nose and his lips served up with pepper and salt in front of him </s>
<s> It took a stout seaman in those days to ply his calling in the Caribbean Gulf </s>
<s> Such a man was Captain John Scarrow, of the ship _Morning Star_, and yet he breathed a long sigh of relief when he heard the splash of the falling anchor and swung at his moorings within a hundred yards of the guns of the citadel of Basseterre </s>
<s> St </s>
<s> Kitt's was his final port of call, and early next morning his bowsprit would be pointed for Old England </s>
<s> He had had enough of those robber-haunted seas </s>
<s> Ever since he had left Maracaibo upon the Main, with his full lading of sugar and red pepper, he had winced at every topsail which glimmered over the violet edge of the tropical sea </s>
<s> He had coasted up the Windward Islands, touching here and there, and assailed continually by stories of villainy and outrage </s>
<s> Captain Sharkey, of the twenty-gun pirate barque, _Happy Delivery_, had passed down the coast, and had littered it with gutted vessels and with murdered men </s>
<s> Dreadful anecdotes were current of his grim pleasantries and of his inflexible ferocity </s>
<s> From the Bahamas to the Main his coal-black barque, with the ambiguous name, had been freighted with death and many things which are worse than death </s>
<s> So nervous was Captain Scarrow, with his new full-rigged ship, and her full and valuable lading, that he struck out to the west as far as Bird's Island to be out of the usual track of commerce </s>
<s> And yet even in those solitary waters he had been unable to shake off sinister traces of Captain Sharkey </s>
<s> One morning they had raised a single skiff adrift upon the face of the ocean </s>
<s> Its only occupant was a delirious seaman, who yelled hoarsely as they hoisted him aboard, and showed a dried-up tongue like a black and wrinkled fungus at the back of his mouth </s>
<s> Water and nursing soon transformed him into the strongest and smartest sailor on the ship </s>
<s> He was from Marblehead, in New England, it seemed, and was the sole survivor of a schooner which had been scuttled by the dreadful Sharkey </s>
<s> For a week Hiram Evanson, for that was his name, had been adrift beneath a tropical sun </s>
<s> Sharkey had ordered the mangled remains of his late captain to be thrown into the boat, "as provisions for the voyage," but the seaman had at once committed it to the deep, lest the temptation should be more than he could bear </s>
<s> He had lived upon his own huge frame until, at the last moment, the _Morning Star_ had found him in that madness which is the precursor of such a death </s>
<s> It was no bad find for Captain Scarrow, for, with a short-handed crew, such a seaman as this big New Englander was a prize worth having </s>
<s> He vowed that he was the only man whom Captain Sharkey had ever placed under an obligation </s>

<s> II THE DEALINGS OF CAPTAIN SHARKEY WITH STEPHEN CRADDOCK Careening was a very necessary operation for the old pirate </s>
<s> On his superior speed he depended both for overhauling the trader and escaping the man-of-war </s>
<s> But it was impossible to retain his sailing qualities unless he periodically--once a year, at the least--cleared his vessel's bottom from the long, trailing plants and crusting barnacles which gather so rapidly in the tropical seas </s>
<s> For this purpose he lightened his vessel, thrust her into some narrow inlet where she would be left high and dry at low water, fastened blocks and tackles to her masts to pull her over on to her bilge, and then scraped her thoroughly from rudder-post to cut-water </s>
<s> During the weeks which were thus occupied the ship was, of course, defenceless; but, on the other hand, she was unapproachable by anything heavier than an empty hull, and the place for careening was chosen with an eye to secrecy, so that there was no great danger </s>
<s> So secure did the captains feel, that it was not uncommon for them, at such times, to leave their ships under a sufficient guard, and to start off in the long-boat, either upon a sporting expedition or, more frequently, upon a visit to some outlying town, where they burned the heads of the women by their swaggering gallantry, or broached pipes of wine in the market square, with a threat to pistol all who would not drink with them </s>
<s> Sometimes they would even appear in cities of the size of Charleston, and walk the streets with their clattering side-arms--an open scandal to the whole law-abiding colony </s>
<s> Such visits were not always paid with impunity </s>
<s> It was one of them, for example, which provoked Lieutenant Maynard to hack off Blackbeard's head, and to spear it upon the end of his bowsprit </s>
<s> But, as a rule, the pirate ruffled and bullied and drabbed without let or hindrance, until it was time for him to go back to his ship once more </s>
<s> There was one pirate, however, who never crossed even the skirts of civilisation, and that was the sinister Sharkey, of the barque _Happy Delivery_ </s>
<s> It may have been from his morose and solitary temper, or, as is more probable, that he knew that his name upon the coast was such that outraged humanity would, against all odds, have thrown themselves upon him, but never once did he show his face in a settlement </s>
<s> When his ship was laid up he would leave her under the charge of Ned Galloway--her New England quartermaster--and would take long voyages in his boat, sometimes, it was said, for the purpose of burying his share of the plunder, and sometimes to shoot the wild oxen of Hispaniola, which, when dressed and barbecued, provided provisions for his next voyage </s>
<s> In the latter case the barque would come round to some pre-arranged spot to pick him up, and take on board what he had shot </s>
<s> There had always been a hope in the islands that Sharkey might be taken on one of these occasions; and at last there came news to Kingston which seemed to justify an attempt upon him </s>
<s> It was brought by an elderly logwood-cutter who had fallen into the pirate's hands, and in some freak of drunken benevolence had been allowed to get away with nothing worse than a slit nose and a drubbing </s>
<s> His account was recent and definite </s>
<s> The _Happy Delivery_ was careening at Torbec on the south-west of Hispaniola </s>
<s> Sharkey, with four men, was buccaneering on the outlying island of La Vache </s>
<s> The blood of a hundred murdered crews was calling out for vengeance, and now at last it seemed as if it might not call in vain </s>
<s> Sir Edward Compton, the high-nosed, red-faced Governor, sitting in solemn conclave with the commandant and the head of the council, was sorely puzzled in his mind as to how he should use this chance </s>
<s> There was no man-of-war nearer than Jamestown, and she was a clumsy old fly-boat, which could neither overhaul the pirate on the seas, nor reach her in a shallow inlet </s>
<s> There were forts and artillerymen both at Kingston and Port Royal, but no soldiers available for an expedition </s>
<s> A private venture might be fitted out--and there were many who had a blood-feud with Sharkey--but what could a private venture do </s>
<s> The pirates were numerous and desperate </s>
<s> As to taking Sharkey and his four companions, that, of course, would be easy if they could get at them; but how were they to get at them on a large well-wooded island like La Vache, full of wild hills and impenetrable jungles </s>
<s> A reward was offered to whoever could find a solution, and that brought a man to the front who had a singular plan, and was himself prepared to carry it out </s>
<s> Stephen Craddock had been that most formidable person, the Puritan gone wrong </s>
<s> Sprung from a decent Salem family, his ill-doing seemed to be a recoil from the austerity of their religion, and he brought to vice all the physical strength and energy with which the virtues of his ancestors had endowed him </s>
<s> He was ingenious, fearless, and exceedingly tenacious of purpose, so that when he was still young, his name became notorious upon the American coast </s>
<s> He was the same Craddock who was tried for his life in Virginia for the slaying of the Seminole Chief, and, though he escaped, it was well known that he had corrupted the witnesses and bribed the judge </s>

<s> Finally he had returned to Jamaica with a considerable fortune, and had settled down to a life of sombre dissipation </s>

<s> Haste was, above all things, necessary, for upon any day the careening might be finished, and the pirates out at sea once more </s>

<s> All that night and the next day the _Happy Delivery_ ran before the easterly trades, and Stephen Craddock lay in the dark of the sail-room working patiently at his wrist-irons </s>

<s> From hour to hour he heard the swish of the water, and knew that the barque must be driving with all set in front of the trade wind </s>
<s> In that case they must be nearly back again to Jamaica by now </s>
<s> What plan could Sharkey have in his head, and what use did he hope to make of him </s>
<s> Craddock set his teeth, and vowed that if he had once been a villain from choice he would, at least, never be one by compulsion </s>
<s> On the second morning Craddock became aware that sail had been reduced in the vessel, and that she was tacking slowly, with a light breeze on her beam </s>
<s> The varying slope of the sail room and the sounds from the deck told his practised senses exactly what she was doing </s>
<s> The short reaches showed him that she was manoeuvring near shore, and making for some definite point </s>
<s> If so, she must have reached Jamaica </s>
<s> But what could she be doing there </s>
<s> And then suddenly there was a burst of hearty cheering from the deck, and then the crash of a gun above his head, and then the answering booming of guns from far over the water </s>
<s> Craddock sat up and strained his ears </s>
<s> Was the ship in action </s>
<s> Only the one gun had been fired, and though many had answered, there were none of the crashings which told of a shot coming home </s>
<s> Then, if it was not an action, it must be a salute </s>
<s> But who would salute Sharkey, the pirate </s>
<s> It could only be another pirate ship which would do so </s>
<s> So Craddock lay back again with a groan, and continued to work at the manacle which still held his right wrist </s>
<s> But suddenly there came the shuffling of steps outside, and he had hardly time to wrap the loose links round his free hand, when the door was unbolted and two pirates came in </s>
<s> "Got your hammer, carpenter" </s>
<s> asked one, whom Craddock recognised as the big quartermaster </s>
<s> "Knock off his leg shackles, then </s>
<s> Better leave the bracelets--he's safer with them on" </s>
<s> With hammer and chisel the carpenter loosened the irons </s>
<s> "What are you going to do with me" </s>
<s> asked Craddock </s>
<s> "Come on deck and you'll see" </s>
<s> The sailor seized him by the arm and dragged him roughly to the foot of the companion </s>
<s> Above him was a square of blue sky cut across by the mizzen gaff, with the colours flying at the peak </s>
<s> But it was the sight of those colours which struck the breath from Stephen Craddock's lips </s>
<s> For there were two of them, and the British ensign was flying above the Jolly Rodger--the honest flag above that of the rogue </s>
<s> For an instant Craddock stopped in amazement, but a brutal push from the pirates behind drove him up the companion ladder </s>
<s> As he stepped out upon deck, his eyes turned up to the main, and there again were the British colours flying above the red pennant, and all the shrouds and rigging were garlanded with streamers </s>
<s> Had the ship been taken, then </s>
<s> But that was impossible, for there were the pirates clustering in swarms along the port bulwarks, and waving their hats joyously in the air </s>
<s> Most prominent of all was the renegade mate, standing on the foc'sle head, and gesticulating wildly </s>
<s> Craddock looked over the side to see what they were cheering at, and then in a flash he saw how critical was the moment </s>
<s> On the port bow, and about a mile off, lay the white houses and forts of Port Royal, with flags breaking out everywhere over their roofs </s>
<s> Right ahead was the opening of the palisades leading to the town of Kingston </s>
<s> Not more than a quarter of a mile off was a small sloop working out against the very slight wind </s>
<s> The British ensign was at her peak, and her rigging was all decorated </s>
<s> On her deck could be seen a dense crowd of people cheering and waving their hats, and the gleam of scarlet told that there were officers of the garrison among them </s>
<s> In an instant, with the quick perception of a man of action, Craddock saw through it all </s>
<s> Sharkey, with that diabolical cunning and audacity which were among his main characteristics, was simulating the part which Craddock would himself have played had he come back victorious </s>
<s> It was in _his_ honour that the salutes were firing and the flags flying </s>
<s> It was to welcome _him_ that this ship with the Governor, the commandant, and the chiefs of the island were approaching </s>
<s> In another ten minutes they would all be under the guns of the _Happy Delivery_, and Sharkey would have won the greatest stake that ever a pirate played for yet </s>
<s> "Bring him forward," cried the pirate captain, as Craddock appeared between the carpenter and the quartermaster </s>
<s> "Keep the ports closed, but clear away the port guns, and stand by for a broadside </s>
<s> Another two cable lengths and we have them" </s>
<s> "They are edging away," said the boatswain </s>
<s> "I think they smell us" </s>
<s> "That's soon set right," said Sharkey, turning his filmy eyes upon Craddock </s>
<s> "Stand there, you--right there, where they can recognise you, with your hand on the guy, and wave your hat to them </s>
<s> Quick, or your brains will be over your coat </s>
<s> Put an inch of your knife into him, Ned </s>
<s> Now, will you wave your hat </s>
<s> Try him again, then </s>
<s> Hey, shoot him </s>
<s> Stop him" </s>
<s> But it was too late </s>
<s> Relying upon the manacles, the quartermaster had taken his hands for a moment off Craddock's arm </s>
<s> In that instant he had flung off the carpenter, and, amid a spatter of pistol bullets, had sprung the bulwarks and was swimming for his life </s>
<s> He had been hit and hit again, but it takes many pistols to kill a resolute and powerful man who has his mind set upon doing something before he dies </s>
<s> He was a strong swimmer, and, in spite of the red trail which he left in the water behind him, he was rapidly increasing his distance from the pirate </s>
<s> "Give me a musket" </s>
<s> cried Sharkey, with a savage oath </s>
<s> He was a famous shot, and his iron nerves never failed him in an emergency </s>
<s> The dark head appearing on the crest of a roller, and then swooping down on the other side, was already half-way to the sloop </s>
<s> Sharkey dwelt long upon his aim before he fired </s>
<s> With the crack of the gun the swimmer reared himself up in the water, waved his hands in a gesture of warning, and roared out in a voice which rang over the bay </s>
<s> Then, as the sloop swung round her head-sails, and the pirate fired an impotent broadside, Stephen Craddock, smiling grimly in his death agony, sank slowly down to that golden couch which glimmered far beneath him </s>
<s> III HOW COPLEY BANKS SLEW CAPTAIN SHARKEY The Buccaneers were something higher than a mere band of marauders </s>
<s> They were a floating republic, with laws, usages, and discipline of their own </s>
<s> In their endless and remorseless quarrel with the Spaniards they had some semblance of right upon their side </s>
<s> Their bloody harryings of the cities of the Main were not more barbarous than the inroads of Spain upon the Netherlands--or upon the Caribs in these same American lands </s>
<s> The chief of the Buccaneers, were he English or French, a Morgan or a Granmont, was still a responsible person, whose country might countenance him, or even praise him, so long as he refrained from any deed which might shock the leathery seventeenth-century conscience too outrageously </s>
<s> Some of them were touched with religion, and it is still remembered how Sawkins threw the dice overboard upon the Sabbath, and Daniel pistolled a man before the altar for irreverence </s>
<s> But there came a day when the fleets of the Buccaneers no longer mustered at the Tortugas, and the solitary and outlawed pirate took their place </s>
<s> Yet even with him the tradition of restraint and of discipline still lingered; and among the early pirates, the Avorys, the Englands, and the Robertses, there remained some respect for human sentiment </s>
<s> They were more dangerous to the merchant than to the seaman </s>
<s> But they in turn were replaced by more savage and desperate men, who frankly recognised that they would get no quarter in their war with the human race, and who swore that they would give as little as they got </s>
<s> Of their histories we know little that is trustworthy </s>
<s> They wrote no memoirs and left no trace, save an occasional blackened and blood-stained derelict adrift upon the face of the Atlantic </s>
<s> Their deeds could only be surmised from the long roll of ships who never made their port </s>
<s> Searching the records of history, it is only here and there in an old-world trial that the veil that shrouds them seems for an instant to be lifted, and we catch a glimpse of some amazing and grotesque brutality behind </s>
<s> Such was the breed of Ned Low, of Gow the Scotchman, and of the infamous Sharkey, whose coal-black barque, the _Happy Delivery_, was known from the Newfoundland Banks to the mouths of the Orinoco as the dark forerunner of misery and of death </s>
<s> There were many men, both among the islands and on the Main, who had a blood feud with Sharkey, but not one who had suffered more bitterly than Copley Banks, of Kingston </s>
<s> Banks had been one of the leading sugar merchants of the West Indies </s>
<s> He was a man of position, a member of the Council, the husband of a Percival, and the cousin of the Governor of Virginia </s>
<s> His two sons had been sent to London to be educated, and their mother had gone over to bring them back </s>
<s> On their return voyage the ship, the _Duchess of Cornwall_, fell into the hands of Sharkey, and the whole family met with an infamous death </s>
<s> Copley Banks said little when he heard the news, but he sank into a morose and enduring melancholy </s>
<s> He neglected his business, avoided his friends, and spent much of his time in the low taverns of the fishermen and seamen </s>
<s> There, amidst riot and devilry, he sat silently puffing at his pipe, with a set face and a smouldering eye </s>
<s> It was generally supposed that his misfortunes had shaken his wits, and his old friends looked at him askance, for the company which he kept was enough to bar him from honest men </s>
<s> From time to time there came rumours of Sharkey over the sea </s>
<s> Sometimes it was from some schooner which had seen a great flame upon the horizon, and approaching to offer help to the burning ship, had fled away at the sight of the sleek, black barque, lurking like a wolf near a mangled sheep </s>
<s> Sometimes it was a frightened trader, which had come tearing in with her canvas curved like a lady's bodice, because she had seen a patched foretopsail rising slowly above the violet water-line </s>
<s> Sometimes it was from a coaster, which had found a waterless Bahama cay littered with sun-dried bodies </s>
<s> Once there came a man who had been mate of a Guineaman, and who had escaped from the pirate's hands </s>
<s> He could not speak--for reasons which Sharkey could best supply--but he could write, and he did write, to the very great interest of Copley Banks </s>
<s> For hours they sat together over the map, and the dumb man pointed here and there to outlying reefs and tortuous inlets, while his companion sat smoking in silence, with his unvarying face and his fiery eyes </s>
<s> One morning, some two years after his misfortunes, Mr Copley Banks strode into his own office with his old air of energy and alertness </s>
<s> The manager stared at him in surprise, for it was months since he had shown any interest in business </s>
<s> "Good morning, Mr Banks" </s>
<s> said he </s>
<s> "Good morning, Freeman </s>
<s> I see that _Ruffling Harry_ is in the Bay" </s>
<s> "Yes, sir; she clears for the Windward Islands on Wednesday" </s>
<s> "I have other plans for her, Freeman </s>
<s> I have determined upon a slaving venture to Whydah" </s>
<s> "But her cargo is ready, sir" </s>
<s> "Then it must come out again, Freeman </s>
<s> My mind is made up, and the _Ruffling Harry_ must go slaving to Whydah" </s>
<s> All argument and persuasion were vain, so the manager had dolefully to clear the ship once more </s>
<s> And then Copley Banks began to make preparations for his African voyage </s>
<s> It appeared that he relied upon force rather than barter for the filling of his hold, for he carried none of those showy trinkets which savages love, but the brig was fitted with eight nine-pounder guns, and racks full of muskets and cutlasses </s>
<s> The after-sailroom next the cabin was transformed into a powder magazine, and she carried as many round shot as a well-found privateer </s>
<s> Water and provisions were shipped for a long voyage </s>
<s> But the preparation of his ship's company was most surprising </s>
<s> It made Freeman, the manager, realise that there was truth in the rumour that his master had taken leave of his senses </s>
<s> For, under one pretext or another, he began to dismiss the old and tried hands, who had served the firm for years, and in their place he embarked the scum of the port--men whose reputations were so vile that the lowest crimp would have been ashamed to furnish them </s>
<s> There was Birthmark Sweetlocks, who was known to have been present at the killing of the logwood-cutters, so that his hideous scarlet disfigurement was put down by the fanciful as being a red afterglow from that great crime </s>
<s> He was first mate, and under him was Israel Martin, a little sun-wilted fellow who had served with Howell Davies at the taking of Cape Coast Castle </s>
<s> The crew were chosen from amongst those whom Banks had met and known in their own infamous haunts, and his own table-steward was a haggard-faced man, who gobbled at you when he tried to talk </s>
<s> His beard had been shaved, and it was impossible to recognise him as the same man whom Sharkey had placed under the knife, and who had escaped to tell his experiences to Copley Banks </s>
<s> These doings were not unnoticed, nor yet uncommented upon in the town of Kingston </s>
<s> The Commandant of the troops--Major Harvey of the Artillery--made serious representations to the Governor </s>
<s> "She is not a trader, but a small warship," said he </s>
<s> "I think it would be as well to arrest Copley Banks and to seize the vessel" </s>
<s> "What do you suspect" </s>
<s> asked the Governor, who was a slow-witted man, broken down with fevers and port wine </s>
<s> "I suspect," said the soldier, "that it is Stede Bonnet over again" </s>
<s> Now, Stede Bonnet was a planter of high reputation and religious character who, from some sudden and overpowering freshet of wildness in his blood, had given up everything in order to start off pirating in the Caribbean Sea </s>
<s> The example was a recent one, and it had caused the utmost consternation in the islands </s>
<s> Governors had before now been accused of being in league with pirates, and of receiving commissions upon their plunder, so that any want of vigilance was open to a sinister construction </s>
<s> "Well, Major Harvey," said he, "I am vastly sorry to do anything which may offend my friend Copley Banks, for many a time have my knees been under his mahogany, but in face of what you say there is no choice for me but to order you to board the vessel and to satisfy yourself as to her character and destination" </s>
<s> So at one in the morning Major Harvey, with a launchful of his soldiers, paid a surprise visit to the _Ruffling Harry_, with the result that they picked up nothing more solid than a hempen cable floating at the moorings </s>
<s> It had been slipped by the brig, whose owner had scented danger </s>
<s> She had already passed the Palisades, and was beating out against the north-east trades on a course for the Windward Passage </s>
<s> When upon the next morning the brig had left Morant Point a mere haze upon the Southern horizon, the men were called aft, and Copley Banks revealed his plans to them </s>
<s> He had chosen them, he said, as brisk boys and lads of spirit, who would rather run some risk upon the sea than starve for a living upon the shore </s>
<s> King's ships were few and weak, and they could master any trader who might come their way </s>
<s> Others had done well at the business, and with a handy, well-found vessel, there was no reason why they should not turn their tarry jackets into velvet coats </s>
<s> If they were prepared to sail under the black flag, he was ready to command them; but if any wished to withdraw, they might have the gig and row back to Jamaica </s>
<s> Four men out of six-and-forty asked for their discharge, went over the ship's side into the boat, and rowed away amidst the jeers and howlings of the crew </s>
<s> The rest assembled aft, and drew up the articles of their association </s>
<s> A square of black tarpaulin had the white skull painted upon it, and was hoisted amidst cheering at the main </s>
<s> Officers were elected, and the limits of their authority fixed </s>
<s> Copley Banks was chosen captain, but, as there are no mates upon a pirate craft, Birthmark Sweetlocks became quartermaster, and Israel Martin the boatswain </s>
<s> There was no difficulty in knowing what was the custom of the brotherhood, for half the men at least had served upon pirates before </s>
<s> Food should be the same for all, and no man should interfere with another man's drink </s>
<s> The captain should have a cabin, but all hands should be welcome to enter it when they chose </s>
<s> All should share and share alike, save only the captain, quartermaster, boatswain, carpenter, and master-gunner, who had from a quarter to a whole share extra </s>
<s> He who saw a prize first should have the best weapon taken out of her </s>
<s> He who boarded her first should have the richest suit of clothes aboard of her </s>
<s> Every man might treat his own prisoner, be it man or woman, after his own fashion </s>
<s> If a man flinched from his gun, the quartermaster should pistol him </s>
<s> These were some of the rules which the crew of the _Ruffling Harry_ subscribed by putting forty-two crosses at the foot of the paper upon which they had been drawn </s>
<s> So a new rover was afloat upon the seas, and her name before a year was over became as well known as that of the _Happy Delivery_ </s>
<s> From the Bahamas to the Leewards, and from the Leewards to the Windwards, Copley Banks became the rival of Sharkey and the terror of traders </s>
<s> For a long time the barque and the brig never met, which was the more singular as the _Ruffling Harry_ was for ever looking in at Sharkey's resorts; but at last one day, when she was passing down the inlet of Coxon's Hole, at the east end of Cuba, with the intention of careening, there was the _Happy Delivery_, with her blocks and tackle-falls already rigged for the same purpose </s>
<s> Copley Banks fired a shotted salute and hoisted the green trumpeter ensign, as the custom was among gentlemen of the sea </s>
<s> Then he dropped his boat and went aboard </s>
<s> Captain Sharkey was not a man of a genial mood, nor had he any kindly sympathy for those who were of the same trade as himself </s>
<s> Copley Banks found him seated astride upon one of the after guns, with his New England quartermaster, Ned Galloway, and a crowd of roaring ruffians standing about him </s>
<s> Yet none of them roared with quite such assurance when Sharkey's pale face and filmy blue eyes were tuned upon him </s>
<s> He was in his shirt-sleeves, with his cambric frills breaking through his open red satin long-flapped vest </s>
<s> The scorching sun seemed to have no power upon his fleshless frame, for he wore a low fur cap, as though it had been winter </s>
<s> A many-coloured band of silk passed across his body and supported a short, murderous sword, while his broad, brass-buckled belt was stuffed with pistols </s>
<s> "Sink you for a poacher" </s>
<s> he cried, as Copley Banks passed over the bulwarks </s>
<s> "I will drub you within an inch of your life, and that inch also </s>
<s> What mean you by fishing in my waters" </s>
<s> Copley Banks looked at him, and his eyes were like those of a traveller who sees his home at last </s>
<s> "I am glad that we are of one mind," said he, "for I am myself of opinion that the seas are not large enough for the two of us </s>
<s> But if you will take your sword and pistols and come upon a sand-bank with me, then the world will be rid of a damned villain, whichever way it goes" </s>
<s> "Now, this is talking" </s>
<s> said Sharkey, jumping off the gun and holding out his hand </s>
<s> "I have not met many who could look John Sharkey in the eyes and speak with a full breath </s>
<s> May the devil seize me if I do not choose you as a consort </s>
<s> But if you play me false, then I will come aboard of you and gut you upon your own poop" </s>
<s> "And I pledge you the same" </s>
<s> said Copley Banks, and so the two pirates became sworn comrades to each other </s>
<s> That summer they went north as far as the Newfoundland Banks, and harried the New York traders and the whale ships from New England </s>
<s> It was Copley Banks who captured the Liverpool ship, _House of Hanover_, but it was Sharkey who fastened her master to the windlass and pelted him to death with empty claret-bottles </s>
<s> Together they engaged the King's ship _Royal Fortune_, which had been sent in search of them, and beat her off after a night action of five hours, the drunken, raving crews fighting naked in the light of the battle-lanterns, with a bucket of rum and a pannikin laid by the tackles of every gun </s>
<s> They ran to Topsail Inlet in North Carolina to refit, and then in the spring they were at the Grand Caicos, ready for a long cruise down the West Indies </s>
<s> By this time Sharkey and Copley Banks had become very excellent friends, for Sharkey loved a whole-hearted villain, and he loved a man of metal, and it seemed to him that the two met in the captain of the _Ruffling Harry_ </s>
<s> It was long before he gave his confidence to him, for cold suspicion lay deep in his character </s>
<s> Never once would he trust himself outside his own ship and away from his own men </s>
<s> But Copley Banks came often on board the _Happy Delivery_, and joined Sharkey in many of his morose debauches, so that at last any lingering misgivings of the latter were set at rest </s>
<s> He knew nothing of the evil that he had done to his new boon companion, for of his many victims how could he remember the woman and the two boys whom he had slain with such levity so long ago </s>
<s> When, therefore, he received a challenge to himself and to his quartermaster for a carouse upon the last evening of their stay at the Caicos Bank he saw no reason to refuse </s>
<s> A well-found passenger ship had been rifled the week before, so their fare was of the best, and after supper five of them drank deeply together </s>
<s> There were the two captains, Birthmark Sweetlocks, Ned Galloway, and Israel Martin, the old buccaneers-man </s>
<s> To wait upon them was the dumb steward, whose head Sharkey split with a glass, because he had been too slow in the filling of it </s>
<s> The quarter-master has slipped Sharkey's pistols away from him, for it was an old joke with him to fire them cross-handed under the table and see who was the luckiest man </s>
<s> It was a pleasantry which had cost his boatswain his leg, so now, when the table was cleared, they would coax Sharkey's weapons away from him on the excuse of the heat, and lay them out of his reach </s>
<s> The captain's cabin of the _Ruffling Harry_ was in a deck-house upon the poop, and a stern-chaser gun was mounted at the back of it </s>
<s> Round shot were racked round the wall, and three great hogsheads of powder made a stand for dishes and for bottles </s>
<s> In this grim room the five pirates sang and roared and drank, while the silent steward still filled up their glasses, and passed the box and the candle round for their tobacco-pipes </s>
<s> Hour after hour the talk became fouler, the voices hoarser, the curses and shoutings more incoherent, until three of the five had closed their blood-shot eyes, and dropped their swimming heads upon the table </s>
<s> Copley Banks and Sharkey were left face to face, the one because he had drunk the least, the other because no amount of liquor would ever shake his iron nerve or warm his sluggish blood </s>

<s> Shake her up </s>
<s> Try her with the mainsail </s>
<s> A trader sailed from Stepney Town With a keg full of gold and a velvet gown </s>

<s> "We did as many as ten ships a week about that time" </s>
<s> "There were a mother and two sons among the passengers </s>

<s> He remembered it, he said, and he added details to prove it </s>

<s> he cried </s>

<s> Then he turned to seize a weapon, but the bight of a rope was cast round him, and in an instant his arms were bound to his side </s>

<s> "Now, you bloody devil," said Copley Banks, softly, "you must listen to what I have to say to you, for they are the last words that you will hear </s>
<s> You are my man now, and I have bought you at a price, for I have given all that a man can give here below, and I have given my soul as well </s>
<s> "To reach you I have had to sink to your level </s>

<s> THE LORD OF CHATEAU NOIR It was in the days when the German armies had broken their way across France, and when the shattered forces of the young Republic had been swept away to the north of the Aisne and to the south of the Loire </s>
<s> Three broad streams of armed men had rolled slowly but irresistibly from the Rhine, now meandering to the north, now to the south, dividing, coalescing, but all uniting to form one great lake round Paris </s>
<s> And from this lake there welled out smaller streams--one to the north, one southward, to Orleans, and a third westward to Normandy </s>
<s> Many a German trooper saw the sea for the first time when he rode his horse girth-deep into the waves at Dieppe </s>
<s> Black and bitter were the thoughts of Frenchmen when they saw this weal of dishonour slashed across the fair face of their country </s>
<s> They had fought and they had been overborne </s>
<s> That swarming cavalry, those countless footmen, the masterful guns--they had tried and tried to make head against them </s>
<s> In battalions their invaders were not to be beaten, but man to man, or ten to ten, they were their equals </s>
<s> A brave Frenchman might still make a single German rue the day that he had left his own bank of the Rhine </s>
<s> Thus, unchronicled amid the battles and the sieges, there broke out another war, a war of individuals, with foul murder upon the one side and brutal reprisal on the other </s>

<s> THE STRIPED CHEST "What do you make of her, Allardyce" </s>

<s> The foremast was still standing, but the foretopsail was flying loose, and the headsails were streaming out in long, white pennons in front of her </s>

<s> A SHADOW BEFORE The 15th of July, 1870, found John Worlington Dodds a ruined gamester of the Stock Exchange </s>
<s> Upon the 17th he was a very opulent man </s>
<s> And yet he had effected the change without leaving the penurious little Irish townlet of Dunsloe, which could have been bought outright for a quarter of the sum which he had earned during the single day that he was within its walls </s>
<s> There is a romance of finance yet to be written, a story of huge forces which are for ever waxing and waning, of bold operations, of breathless suspense, of agonised failure, of deep combinations which are baffled by others still more subtle </s>
<s> The mighty debts of each great European Power stand like so many columns of mercury, for ever rising and falling to indicate the pressure upon each </s>
<s> He who can see far enough into the future to tell how that ever-varying column will stand to-morrow is the man who has fortune within his grasp </s>
<s> John Worlington Dodds had many of the gifts which lead a speculator to success </s>
<s> He was quick in observing, just in estimating, prompt and fearless in acting </s>
<s> But in finance there is always the element of luck, which, however one may eliminate it, still remains, like the blank at roulette, a constantly present handicap upon the operator </s>
<s> And so it was that Worlington Dodds had come to grief </s>
<s> On the best advices he had dabbled in the funds of a South American Republic in the days before South American Republics had been found out </s>
<s> The Republic defaulted, and Dodds lost his money </s>
<s> He had bulled the shares of a Scotch railway, and a four months' strike had hit him hard </s>
<s> He had helped to underwrite a coffee company in the hope that the public would come along upon the feed and gradually nibble away some of his holding, but the political sky had been clouded and the public had refused to invest </s>
<s> Everything which he had touched had gone wrong, and now, on the eve of his marriage, young, clear-headed, and energetic, he was actually a bankrupt had his creditors chosen to make him one </s>
<s> But the Stock Exchange is an indulgent body </s>
<s> What is the case of one to-day may be that of another to-morrow, and everyone is interested in seeing that the stricken man is given time to rise again </s>
<s> So the burden of Worlington Dodds was lightened for him; many shoulders helped to bear it, and he was able to go for a little summer tour into Ireland, for the doctors had ordered him rest and change of air to restore his shaken nervous system </s>
<s> Thus it was that upon the 15th of July, 1870, he found himself at his breakfast in the fly-blown coffee-room of the "George Hotel" in the market square of Dunsloe </s>
<s> It is a dull and depressing coffee-room, and one which is usually empty, but on this particular day it was as crowded and noisy as that of any London hotel </s>
<s> Every table was occupied, and a thick smell of fried bacon and of fish hung in the air </s>
<s> Heavily booted men clattered in and out, spurs jingled, riding-crops were stacked in corners, and there was a general atmosphere of horse </s>
<s> The conversation, too, was of nothing else </s>
<s> From every side Worlington Dodds heard of yearlings, of windgalls, of roarers, of spavins, of cribsuckers, of a hundred other terms which were as unintelligible to him as his own Stock Exchange jargon would have been to the company </s>
<s> He asked the waiter for the reason of it all, and the waiter was an astonished man that there should be any man in this world who did not know it </s>
<s> "Shure it's the Dunsloe horse fair, your honour--the greatest horse-fair in all Oireland </s>
<s> It lasts for a wake, and the folk come from far an' near--from England an' Scotland an' iverywhere </s>
<s> If you look out of the winder, your honour, you'll see the horses, and it's asy your honour's conscience must be, or you wouldn't slape so sound that the creatures didn't rouse you with their clatter" </s>

<s> THE KING OF THE FOXES It was after a hunting dinner, and there were as many scarlet coats as black ones round the table </s>
<s> The conversation over the cigars had turned, therefore, in the direction of horses and horsemen, with reminiscences of phenomenal runs where foxes had led the pack from end to end of a county, and been overtaken at last by two or three limping hounds and a huntsman on foot, while every rider in the field had been pounded </s>
<s> As the port circulated the runs became longer and more apocryphal, until we had the whips inquiring their way and failing to understand the dialect of the people who answered them </s>
<s> The foxes, too, became mere eccentric, and we had foxes up pollard willows, foxes which were dragged by the tail out of horses' mangers, and foxes which had raced through an open front door and gone to ground in a lady's bonnet-box </s>
<s> The master had told one or two tall reminiscences, and when he cleared his throat for another we were all curious, for he was a bit of an artist in his way, and produced his effects in a _crescendo_ fashion </s>
<s> His face wore the earnest, practical, severely accurate expression which heralded some of his finest efforts </s>
<s> "It was before I was master," said he </s>
<s> "Sir Charles Adair had the hounds at that time, and then afterwards they passed to old Lathom, and then to me </s>
<s> It may possibly have been just after Lathom took them over, but my strong impression is that it was in Adair's time </s>
<s> That would be early in the seventies--about seventy-two, I should say </s>
<s> "The man I mean has moved to another part of the country, but I daresay that some of you can remember him </s>
<s> Danbury was the name--Walter Danbury, or Wat Danbury, as the people used to call him </s>
<s> He was the son of old Joe Danbury, of High Ascombe, and when his father died he came into a very good thing, for his only brother was drowned when the _Magna Charta_ foundered, so he inherited the whole estate </s>
<s> It was but a few hundred acres, but it was good arable land, and those were the great days of farming </s>
<s> Besides, it was freehold, and a yeoman farmer without a mortgage was a warmish man before the great fall in wheat came </s>
<s> Foreign wheat and barbed wire--those are the two curses of this country, for the one spoils the farmer's work and the other spoils his play </s>
<s> "This young Wat Danbury was a very fine fellow, a keen rider, and a thorough sportsman, but his head was a little turned at having come, when so young, into a comfortable fortune, and he went the pace for a year or two </s>
<s> The lad had no vice in him, but there was a hard-drinking set in the neighbourhood at that time, and Danbury got drawn in among them; and, being an amiable fellow who liked to do what his friends were doing, he very soon took to drinking a great deal more than was good for him </s>

<s> The New Catacomb "Look here, Burger," said Kennedy, "I do wish that you would confide in me" </s>
<s> The two famous students of Roman remains sat together in Kennedy's comfortable room overlooking the Corso </s>
<s> The night was cold, and they had both pulled up their chairs to the unsatisfactory Italian stove which threw out a zone of stuffiness rather than of warmth </s>

<s> THE DEBUT OF BIMBASHI JOYCE It was in the days when the tide of Mahdism, which had swept in such a flood from the great Lakes and Darfur to the confines of Egypt, had at last come to its full, and even begun, as some hoped, to show signs of a turn </s>

<s> A FOREIGN OFFICE ROMANCE There are many folk who knew Alphonse Lacour in his old age </s>
<s> From about the time of the Revolution of '48 until he died in the second year of the Crimean War he was always to be found in the same corner of the Cafe de Provence, at the end of the Rue St </s>
